Biome Italic (biome-italic.ttf)

cmap

00AD

Soft hyphen 00AD in cmap table.

Soft hyphen is often used in web and in professional print publishing software like Adobe InDesign.

Pass

Biome Light Regular (biome-light.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Biome-Light', Everything looks good.

Biome Light Regular (biome-light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Biome' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Biome Light'.

Biome Light Italic (biome-lightitalic.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Biome' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light Italic' = NID 1 'Biome Light' + 'Space' + NID 2 'Italic'.

Biome Italic (biome-italic.ttf)

name

Mac NID 6

Mac NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Biome-Italic', Everything looks good.

Pass

Check gasp table Default.

gasp table default is:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True
and should be:
Grid-fit = True, Do gray = True, Symmetric grid-fit = True, Symmetric smoothing = True

Info

Biome Light Regular (biome-light.ttf)

post

PostScript names

Postscript names should not be longer then 29 characters. May cause issues in PDF.

Every PostScript name is fine.

Pass

sinf

OK: There is a subs and sinf feature in the font.
